opt3dmat - Wrapper for optical imaging analysis

*Opt3dmat.m *Dr. Kyle Mathewson - June 8, 2013 - Translation of Gabriele Gratton's opt3d_fast_v2.f90

Contents

  • Setup workspace global variables
  • run script to load parameter maxima (maybe take out)
  • load .prm file
  • set some parameters - BUILD INTO GUI
  • setup the progress bar
  • load .loc file
  • Compute the bananas for each slice
  • Transform
  • Plot coverage bananas
  • Convert lookup tables to voxel lists
  • load data from p_pod
  • Create data brik from .001 files, for each voxel average the channels data going in, for single data point

Setup workspace global variables

cd C:\Dropbox\experiments\Optical\OPTLAB\opt3d\Opt3DMat0.3
clear all
close all
global prm maxprm loc look vox

run script to load parameter maxima (maybe take out)

prm_max

load .prm file

[fname_prm, pname_prm] = uigetfile('*.prm','Select an opt3d .prm file:');
fname_prm = [pname_prm fname_prm];
readprm(fname_prm);
% readprm('files\rop_pilot.prm'); %debug
% readprm('E:\Data\emm\o3d\ALL_timefreq.prm'); %debug

set some parameters - BUILD INTO GUI

prm.nsubj = 1;
prm.slices = 2:2:192;  %go by 2 (e.g. 2:2:192)
prm.nslice = length(prm.slices);
prm.modeltype = 2; %1 geometric, 2 physical
prm.idata = 1; %type of data, 1 if acdc, 2 if phase
prm.mapdir = 1;
prm.dstcrit = 2;
prm.dstcrit2 = 4.5;

setup the progress bar

slice_plural = 's';
sub_plural = 's';
if prm.nslice == 1;
    slice_plural = '';
end
if prm.nsubj == 1;
    sub_plural = '';
end

load .loc file

[fname_loc, pname_loc] = uigetfile('*.loc','Select an opt3d .loc file:');
fname_loc = [pname_prm fname_loc];
readloc(fname_loc);
% readloc('files\rop_pilot.loc'); %debug
% readloc('E:\Data\emm\o3d\ALL.loc'); %debug

Sub 1. Done.

Transform

look.coverage_slices = permute(look.coverage_slices,[3 1 2]);
look.log_chan_per_vox = permute(look.log_chan_per_vox,[3 1 2]);
look.log_weight_per_vox = permute(look.log_weight_per_vox,[3 1 2]);

Plot coverage bananas

plot_bananas

Convert lookup tables to voxel lists

convert2vox

load data from p_pod

import_ppod
% import_avm

Create data brik from .001 files, for each voxel average the channels data going in, for single data point

for i_block = 1:data(1).n_blocks
    data(i_block).PC.vox = zeros(length(data(i_block).time_stamps),vox.nvox);
    for i_vox = 1:vox.nvox
        fprintf(['Voxel Number: ' num2str(i_vox) '. \n'])
        if prm.modeltype == 1
            data(i_block).PC.vox(:,i_vox) = mean(   data(i_block).PC.dc(:,vox.chans{i_vox}),2);
        elseif prm.modeltype == 2
            data(i_block).PC.vox(:,i_vox) = mean( data(i_block).PC.dc(:,vox.chans{i_vox}).*repmat(vox.weights{i_vox},[length(data(i_block).time_stamps),1]),2);
        end
    end
end

plot_block = 2;
figure; imagesc(data(plot_block).time_stamps,1:vox.nvox,data(plot_block).PC.vox', [-1 1]);
hold on; plot(data(plot_block).time_stamps,data(plot_block).triggers*vox.nvox,'k');
